{"nick":"joepie91","message":"not just for direct dependencies, but also for deps of deps","date":"2016-08-09T11:20:31.980Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"arlekin","message":"joepie91: oh i see","date":"2016-08-09T11:20:41.539Z","type":"message"}

{"nick":"joepie91","message":"meaning you always get the same version that you originally installed","date":"2016-08-09T11:20:48.010Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"joepie91","message":"Sinopia is a sort of 'fake registry' that you can run on your own infrastructure","date":"2016-08-09T11:20:55.946Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"joepie91","message":"that passes through your requests to the actual NPM","date":"2016-08-09T11:21:04.428Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"LeftWing","reason":"Remote host closed the connection","date":"2016-08-09T11:21:05.141Z","type":"quit"}
{"nick":"joepie91","message":"and caches things locally","date":"2016-08-09T11:21:07.062Z","type":"message"}

{"nick":"joepie91","message":"combining the two gets you (almost) completely reproducible dependencies","date":"2016-08-09T11:21:27.011Z","type":"message"}
